  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_3245ae80-ebd5-4432-9bdd-86740255cd3f'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer735936327" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8791079856713575338"><b> ‘More Than’ 5 stars!!!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/ec801d7d-bc29-427e-aeb9-77e4aaf38704_zpsb4619789.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403601880i/10116650.jpg' alt=' photo ec801d7d-bc29-427e-aeb9-77e4aaf38704_zpsb4619789.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><i>
  <blockquote>Love has no limits. No boundaries. No time. It’s eternal. Forever.</blockquote>
</i><br/>This book was <b>perfection</b>.<br/>This series is <b>amazing</b>.<br/>I randomly stumbled on a friends review of a new release called <i>More Than This</i> last year and thought I’d give it a go. I fell in love with that book. Each book in the series has been better than the last, and this is my favorite by far. I have been so excited to read about Lucy ever since I met her. But Cam… oh my Cam. How did I overlook him in the firs</span>
  <span id="freeText8791079856713575338" style="display:none"><b> ‘More Than’ 5 stars!!!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/ec801d7d-bc29-427e-aeb9-77e4aaf38704_zpsb4619789.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403601880i/10116650.jpg" alt=" photo ec801d7d-bc29-427e-aeb9-77e4aaf38704_zpsb4619789.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><i>
  <blockquote>Love has no limits. No boundaries. No time. It’s eternal. Forever.</blockquote>
</i><br>This book was <b>perfection</b>.<br>This series is <b>amazing</b>.<br>I randomly stumbled on a friends review of a new release called <i>More Than This</i> last year and thought I’d give it a go. I fell in love with that book. Each book in the series has been better than the last, and this is my favorite by far. I have been so excited to read about Lucy ever since I met her. But Cam… oh my Cam. How did I overlook him in the first 3 books? I’ve always loved Logan best, but now… now it’s all about Cam! <br><br>Cameron is one of those perfect guys. Loving, caring, supportive. I loved seeing him in the beginning stages of their relationship. He was Lucy’s strength, her rock. She needed that. He wasn’t just there for her, he was there for her brothers. You will not be able to read this book and not fall in love with Cam. It just can’t happen. <br><i>
  <blockquote>Cameron is an artist. He’s an athlete. He’s an unbelievably respectful son. Above all that, Cameron has a heart the size of the ocean.</blockquote>
</i><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/81f08b38-d742-43cf-9bc0-f1e2da755f9f_zpsf8981c70.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403601881i/10116651.jpg" alt=" photo 81f08b38-d742-43cf-9bc0-f1e2da755f9f_zpsf8981c70.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The weight of the world was put on Lucy’s shoulders after her mother’s passing. What would she have done without Cam’s love, support and devotion? It’s hard to tell. Watching the two of them fall in love was so beautiful. Jay has this way about writing the sweetest, most emotional scenes, but there is also so much humor laced in. Getting to experience the beginning of Cam and Lucy was wonderful. All the ‘first’s’ that come with young love.<br><i>
  <blockquote> “Is this… I mean…. have you ever been kissed before?” My head shakes frantically. I can’t control it.<br>His face lights up.<br>I don’t know why he’s happy that he’s trying to make out with a pajama wearing, frozen, virgin kisser. That doesn’t sound like happy times at all.<br>“So I’m your first?” I nod again. The same speed as before. That’s it- I’ve lost control of all bodily function.<br>“I like that.”</blockquote>
</i><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/03faefd1-6cd3-4978-bb1a-6e32a2f3b794_zps08a37c43.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403601881i/10116652.jpg" alt=" photo 03faefd1-6cd3-4978-bb1a-6e32a2f3b794_zps08a37c43.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“You make my world stop, Lucy.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b> Cam and Lucy don’t have the normal high school relationship. They know early on that they are it for each other. Through all the struggles, loss and life’s challenges, one thing stays consistent. They have each other. <br><br>Through highschool and college, their relationship has some ups and downs. I’d love to say that it stayed 100% perfect, easy etc, but I would be lying. It was hard sometimes, but thats real. Lucy and Cam go through their fair share of heartbreak and conflict. Your heart will shatter, you will cry, but it will be worth every second of heartache. <br><br>They both want forever with each other. Is forever possible?<br><i>
  <blockquote>“It’s the sunrise and sunset. He says it reminds him of our love. Because it’s eternal- the rise and fall of the sun. It’s forever. Just like us.”</blockquote>
</i><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/da1cd66a-1334-40f4-8549-44c9b2170d51_zpsaa16e31a.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403601881i/10116653.jpg" alt=" photo da1cd66a-1334-40f4-8549-44c9b2170d51_zpsaa16e31a.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>A book like this is so difficult to review. I want to add in so much, but I don’t want to spoil anything. I highlighted pages and pages worth of quotes. Here are some of the things you have to look forward to… <br><br>√ Mark- EVERYTHING about Mark. <br>√ The river and the cabin ♥ <br>√ Lucy’s brothers <br>√ Clitorusaurus-Rex<br>√ Lucy’s whore comments <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The first time was the best… sweet and innocent Lucy getting jealous ;) <br><i>“Did you call me?” she asks Cam.<br>And a fire burns in the pit of my stomach. I know what the fire is now. It’s called jealousy.<br>“Yeah.” I glare at her. “He called you a whore.”</i> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>√ Puncy Cam<br>√ Aladdin speech<br>√ The sex… <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ <br><b><i>“PULL MY HAIR!” I’d laugh but I’m so fucking close to coming that if I moved wrong, I would. <br>“PULL IT!” “Okay!” I yell. I reach up and tug her hair.<br>“FUCK YEAH, BABY!” She’s on all fours, on the floor of the living room. “GRAB MY TITS!” I reach around and do what she asks, trying not to lose the rhythm of my pumps. Fuck, I love her like this. <br>“RUB MY CLIT!” “I DONT’ HAVE ANYMORE HANDS!”</i></b> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>√ Operations Mayhem or Ho-perations Whore-hem<br>√ Drunk Lucy<br>√ The first times… <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <i>“It’s kind of hot. I actually enjoyed it. Until you know… the whole funky spunk in my mouth thing.”</i>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br> Thats just a taste of the greatness you have to look forward to when reading this book! <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/807d3370-c09f-43d0-aa36-abd3afe3d57a_zps86bb4f23.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403602085i/10116680.jpg" alt=" photo 807d3370-c09f-43d0-aa36-abd3afe3d57a_zps86bb4f23.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>So lets wrap it up…. <i>More than Forever</i> is an emotional, hilarious, beautiful, heart breaking, and a healing tale of a <b>first love</b>, an <b>only love</b>, a <b>FOREVER love</b>. It’s a story of love, loss and hope. A story that will make you believe in real and true love. All the humor evens out the emotional aspect perfectly. This is a book (and series) that you don’t want to miss out on it. I’m being serious here. If you haven’t read these books, drop what your doing and do it! Promise you won’t regret it! ♥ ♥ ♥<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%205/adbb8dda-f88b-449c-887d-1854ee4f4918_zpsbb935179.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403601881i/10116654.jpg" alt=" photo adbb8dda-f88b-449c-887d-1854ee4f4918_zpsbb935179.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <blockquote>There is a love so fierce it cannot be measured. <br>A heart so strong it will never slow.<br>There is a promise so sure it can never lie.<br>And we promise that love forever.<br> Forever and always.</blockquote>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/fbfe5257-5c23-4da3-b325-31eaf8f2110a_zpsd0802295.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1399922023i/9610271.jpg" alt=" photo fbfe5257-5c23-4da3-b325-31eaf8f2110a_zpsd0802295.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alexis *Reality Bites*" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alexis *Reality Bites*" href="/user/show/5587514-alexis-reality-bites">Alexis *Reality Bites*</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer736139090" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12575292074770183402"><b>
  <u>Full Review Posted 7-11-14</u>
</b> <br/>5 STAR READ<br/>Genre: New Adult Romance<br/><br/>This is the first book in a good while that as soon as I finished..I wanted to go back to the beginning and start all over. <br/><b>I'm in love with <i>love</i>!</b> <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405060678i/10333327.jpg' alt=' photo MTFCOLLAGEfinal1_zps01147328.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Jay McLean navigates readers on an emotional journey. Full with plenty of ups, downs and shake ups that move you, whether it’s to amuse you, bemuse you or just shatter you in to pieces. More Than Forever hits you at all angles: death, life, love, hate, rejection, acceptance and change t</span>
  <span id="freeText12575292074770183402" style="display:none"><b>
  <u>Full Review Posted 7-11-14</u>
</b> <br>5 STAR READ<br>Genre: New Adult Romance<br><br>This is the first book in a good while that as soon as I finished..I wanted to go back to the beginning and start all over. <br><b>I'm in love with <i>love</i>!</b> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405060678i/10333327.jpg" alt=" photo MTFCOLLAGEfinal1_zps01147328.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Jay McLean navigates readers on an emotional journey. Full with plenty of ups, downs and shake ups that move you, whether it’s to amuse you, bemuse you or just shatter you in to pieces. More Than Forever hits you at all angles: death, life, love, hate, rejection, acceptance and change to name a few.<br><br>Unlike the previous books in this series More Than Forever takes you back in time. It starts with a young Lucy, only 15, a girl carrying the weight of the world on her shoulders. A world that is about to be forever changed…<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405060375i/10333290.jpg" alt=" photo MTFCamquote1_zpsf8a21901.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Cameron has been assisting with little league, when practice ends he spots her in the stands, sitting on a bench reading with her kindle in one hand as her foot gently rocks a stroller to soothe baby Lachlan. That’s when it happens, thunder bolt, cupid’s arrow, love at first sight, whatever it is you would like to call it. He falls and he falls hard.<br><br>Cam quickly realizes that not everything is how it seems. He comes to understand that Lucy is going through her daily routine which pretty much has her caring for her younger brothers because her mother is ill and no longer able to do so. She is literally living on auto pilot. <br><br>When tragedy strikes he is the only one who sees the <b>real</b> Lucy and it is then that he learns her dark secret. Cam takes it upon himself to help out with the boys. Without so much as a second glance Luce continues to do her part and care for her siblings only<b> now</b> she has help; whether she wants it or not.<br><br>With a big heart and a calming presence Cam manages to become a big part of Lucy’s life. Before she even realizes it he soon holds a place in her heart. <b>A permanent place. A forever place.</b><br><br><i>
  <b>“He’s fierce.” <br>His brows rise. “Fierce?”<br>“Yeah. The way he protects me. It’s fierce. He’s fierce.”</b>
</i> <br>-Lucy talking to her dad about Cam<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405060678i/10333328.jpg" alt=" photo MTFCOLLAGE3FINAL_zpsc8374e58.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When I entered Lucy and Cam’s <b>'More'</b> world I had no idea what to expect, we’ve only had small glimpses of Cam and hilarious doses of a drunk Lucy in prior books. MTF has you at the forefront of their lives. What I found so beautiful about this story <b>is</b> its<b> two</b> main <b>characters</b> and the ease at which they connected at such a young age. <br><br><i>
  <b>“You make me want to try.” He whispers in my ear.</b>
</i> -Cam <br><br>It was said that Cam has a heart the size of the ocean and I must say I totally agree. He was able to take Lucy’s crumbling world and rebuild it minus any judgment. Because seeing Lucy at her lowest point made him run towards her <b>NOT</b> away.<br><br>I really <b>really</b> enjoyed the way their relationship blossomed from their teens and carried in to adulthood. It was wonderfully and flawlessly executed. You get the innocence of first love, the tenderness of a first kiss, the loss of virginity, the transition to college, new responsibilities of juggling school, work and a relationship. <b>All</b> of these pivotal life changes occur. Each has an impact on their relationship, some good, some not so good.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405060375i/10333292.jpg" alt=" photo MTFCamQUOTESPICFINAL1_zpsf7ac7cbf.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b> ‘As much as it hurts to admit, things have changed. I don’t know if its me, or him, or both of us.’</b>
</i> -Lucy<br><br> After 5 years of being together Lucy and Cam experience some horrible growing pains. I felt so bad for them. But I also felt that it was captured honestly. What I thought was important during this time is how never..not for one second did I doubt their love for one another. Still, like every other couple they experience challenges. Nothing in life is perfect, right. After all its how we overcome and learn from those challenges in life that truly matter.<br><br>Take the journey! Come live, learn and love with Cam and Lucy in More Than Forever!<br><br><i>
  <b>‘Sometimes we talk. Most of the time it’s just me talking, trying to make her laugh. Trying to gift my ears with the sound that makes my world stop.’ </b>
</i> –Cam<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405060375i/10333291.jpg" alt=" photo mtfcollagefinal2_zps4e869bb8.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>
  <u>My Sweet and Sour</u>
</b><br><u>My Sweet</u>- My Forever, by Cameron Loves You More Annnnd Lucas!! Jay, give us MORE Lucas!!!<br><u>My Sour</u>- Wellll, it begins with an R ends with a Y. <br><br>WAIT! To those who read the book already…Did anyone peep this…how it was said that Tom made the counter higher in the kitchen on purpose…because he was described as tall but that’s not why it was so he could sex up his wife. *wiggles eyebrows* GREAT inside joke he shared with his wife. Too cute!<br><br><u>My Thoughts</u><br>I LOVED IT! If I had to describe the writing I would say it's beautifully written, fantastically witty and totally raw. Although Lucy suffered a big loss in More Than Forever it did not over shadow the story. Jay McLean manages to find a balance also nothing drags along. Just when I thought the book was about to slip in to a predictable story line McLean hit the brakes and<b> surprised </b>me. That scene when Cam finally puts two and two together....<br><br>One thing about McLean’s style is that she likes to show case relationships. Not too many authors have the ability to write in the parents <b>the way</b> McLean does. She makes you wish your parents were that cool. And if your parents are already that cool, well, you’re just that damn lucky.<br><br>Smart mouth Lucy? I felt like she was in and out. Sometimes I’d expect something crazy to fly out her mouth and then I’d remember most times she was drunk when that happened in previous books. In MTF we get to know the many sides of Lucy. <br><br><b>My Reviews for the other books in this series</b><br><b>Book #1 More Than This-</b> <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/661614271?book_show_action=false">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a><br><b>Book #2 More Than Her-</b> <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/671773495?book_show_action=false">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a><br><b>Book #3 More Than Him-</b> <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/771157367?book_show_action=false">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a> <br><br>NOTE: Just added a link to my recent interview with author Jay Mclean, in it we discuss her characters. Who was the most fun to write? Will Heidi's story EVER be told? And what was her biggest challenge while writing<b> this book?</b> Find out in the link posted below. <br><b>My recent interview with Jay McLean:</b> <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://realitybites-letsgetlost.blogspot.com/2014/06/author-spotlight-interview-and-giveaway.html">http://realitybites-letsgetlost.blogs...</a><br><br><br><br><u>My Ratings</u><br><b>Characters-</b> Lovable, Sweet and Witty<br><b>Writing Style-</b> Beautiful and Raw<br><b>Plot/Storyline-</b> A love story with two teens as they go from youth to adults facing life’s many challenges along the way.<br><b>Steam Factor-</b> High/Steamy on a scale of 1-10 I say 7<br><b>Entertainment Level-</b> High, I found myself enthralled!<br><b>Overall-</b> I LOVED IT!!! READ IT!!<br><b><br>Now go forth and read. Then come tell us about it on Goodreads!</b><br><b>For more reviews got to:</b> <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.realitybites-letsgetlost.blogspot.com">www.realitybites-letsgetlost.blogspot...</a> <br><b>Like us on Facebook:</b> <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.facebook.com/realitybitesletsgetlost">www.facebook.com/realitybitesletsgetlost</a><br><br><br><br><br><b> Me Prior to the book release -October 2013</b><br><b>Ummmmm...how am I just now seeing this?????</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381162857ra/4419184.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mcfc3jxHIm1qkomroo1_500_zps892f1738.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>Cam and Lucy? HELL YES!!!</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380852307ra/3135368.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mqnw1qw3wY1s5vi0bo1_500_zps536cf355.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<div id="review_2405955611" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2405955611" />
    <a title="mel ☽" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/41864935-mel"><img alt="mel ☽" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1605046766p2/41864935.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2405955611?book_show_action=true">Jul 26, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="mel ☽" class="user" itemprop="url" name="mel ☽" href="/user/show/41864935-mel">mel ☽</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41864935-mel?shelf=2019-favorites">2019-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41864935-mel?shelf=all-time-favorites">all-time-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41864935-mel?shelf=angst">angst</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41864935-mel?shelf=book-boyfriends">book-boyfriends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41864935-mel?shelf=emotional">emotional</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41864935-mel?shelf=favorite-heroes">favorite-heroes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41864935-mel?shelf=im-so-single">im-so-single</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41864935-mel?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41864935-mel?shelf=funny">funny</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/41864935-mel?shelf=grovelling">grovelling</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2405955611" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12932749332852210708"><b>reread (oct 2020)</b> — <i>still 5 stars</i><br/><br/>i was already single but after rereading this, i am now <b>PAINFULLY</b> single. <br/><br/>y'all. Cameron? Lucy-? ugh GOD. okay. so i was feeling some type of way again right? so on a whim, i decided to reread this again just cuz i've been feeling like a robot lately so i had to make sure i'm human but <i>anyways</i>- this was painful but in a good way (?). <br/><br/>the UNCONDITIONAL love?<br/>passion? the emotions??<br/>family relationships & friendships?<br/>little Lucas, Logan, and Leo??? Lachlan?!<br/>the DRAAA</span>
  <span id="freeText12932749332852210708" style="display:none"><b>reread (oct 2020)</b> — <i>still 5 stars</i><br><br>i was already single but after rereading this, i am now <b>PAINFULLY</b> single. <br><br>y'all. Cameron? Lucy-? ugh GOD. okay. so i was feeling some type of way again right? so on a whim, i decided to reread this again just cuz i've been feeling like a robot lately so i had to make sure i'm human but <i>anyways</i>- this was painful but in a good way (?). <br><br>the UNCONDITIONAL love?<br>passion? the emotions??<br>family relationships &amp; friendships?<br>little Lucas, Logan, and Leo??? Lachlan?!<br>the DRAAAMAAA?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1519008875ra/25084211.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>to be honest with you guys, i don't think i've ever read any other books like this where the MCs are <i>that</i> in love with each other that i 100% believe that if they ever break up, they'd forever stay single until they get together again. like, it's simply impossible for them to be with other people. this type of unconditional love is ~ <b>
  <i>unmatched</i>
</b> ~<br><br>Cameron and Lucy are each others' first EVERYTHING- literally, <i>everything</i>. if you know what i mean. and even when they break up, they're still a couple. <br><br>but anyways imma just show y'all why this book made me feel single:<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>"I feel like I've loved you for eternity, and it's not even close to long enough"</blockquote>
</b><br><br>Spain without the S.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>"Because it's eternal, the rise and fall of the sun. It's forever. Just like us"</blockquote>
</b><br><br>Liam Payne but make Liam silent.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>"There is a love so fierce it cannot be measured. A heart so strong it will never slow. There is a promise so sure it can never lie. And we promise that love forever. Forever and always."</blockquote>
</b><br><br>bro i just- <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1603504153i/30279829._SX540_.jpg" width="380" height="230" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>GOD, <b>I AM SO SINGLE</b>.<br><br>and y'all know what i just realized? this takes place around the time Leo met Mia, meaning Lucas and Logan were their asshole selves.. huh. hmm... what to do with that information..<br><br>➵ <b>
  <u>OW drama</u>
</b><br>you know the saying, "love makes you stupid"? well, that's what happened here because Cameron was kind of an <b>accidental dumbass</b>. he was so in love with Lucy, he didn't even know his classmate/coworker, <b>Roxie</b>, was flirting and trying to lowkey steal him away. he even drew her and then Lucy saw that he drew her and that scene broke my heart!!!<br><br>honestly tho, this is one of the rare moments where i didn't find this drama annoying because the drama was GOOD. i couldn't stop reading it because i love when H fucks up, h gets mad and don't forgive them and then H grovels multiple times. love that dynamic because im bored af so i need this type of messy drama.<br><br>* * * <br><br>and can we talk about this line by our girl Lucy?<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"I hope your dick gets whore poisoning and shrivels to its death! And then I hope all the girls see it and laugh at you! And then I hope it falls off! You can stare down at it and cry like a little bitch, just like you did when your pet hamster died!"</b>
</blockquote><br><br>~ <b>
  <i>iconic</i>
</b> ~ <br><br><b>Lucy and Cam are legit soulmates</b>. no doubt about that. they're one of those rare book couples i read where their love is so passionate and emotional that whatever they feel, i feel it even more. <br><br>they're the kind of fictional couple that really make you go... <i>damn, i'm so <s>painfully</s> single</i>, even if you're in a relationship.<br><br>✧—— ✧ *⋆* ✧ * ⋆* ✧ * ⋆* ✧——⋆✧<br><br><b>first read (july 2019):</b> — <i>5 stars</i><br>note to past self: damn b who hurt you back then?<br><br><i>“You make my world stop, Lucy.”</i><br>pfft i wish someone would say that to me but nope the world is full of fuckboys and dumbasses plenty of fish in the sea but there’s also plenty of trash, if ya know what I mean. <br><br>Is Cameron one or both of those things? Of course not! That man is literally perfect! <br>Reading through Cam and Lucy’s awkward teenage love (this the best part btw) blossom to something mature and passionate is the best thing ever. <br><br>This is honestly the cutest shit I’ve ever read and I felt every emotion. I was smiling like a goof the first half and I was laughing and crying like a baby in the second half. I just honestly love this book and this is definitely gonna be added in my all-time favorites.</span>
  <a data-text-id="12932749332852210708" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer972650616" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17132393887431722524">5--<b><i>Our</i> Forever</b>--Stars!!<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380409169ra/800993.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Cam Gordon...you are <b>PERFECTION</b>! <br/><br/>I fell in love with Lucy and Cam in the other books in the series. To say that I was scared to read their story is a gross understatement. In my eyes they were perfect. <br/><br/><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"You're my art, Luce. My heart."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br/>The first half of the book...watching Cam and Lucy fall in love....there are no words. Cam came in to Lucy's life when she needed somone the most. When she was at her lowest. He gave her strength when she had none. He gave her <b>
  <i>h</i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText17132393887431722524" style="display:none">5--<b><i>Our</i> Forever</b>--Stars!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380409169ra/800993.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Cam Gordon...you are <b>PERFECTION</b>! <br><br>I fell in love with Lucy and Cam in the other books in the series. To say that I was scared to read their story is a gross understatement. In my eyes they were perfect. <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"You're my art, Luce. My heart."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>The first half of the book...watching Cam and Lucy fall in love....there are no words. Cam came in to Lucy's life when she needed somone the most. When she was at her lowest. He gave her strength when she had none. He gave her <b>
  <i>hope</i>
</b>!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403532428i/10104493.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Cam was Lucy's rock. He was a hero to Lucy's brother's. He was light in Lucy's dark. They fell in love at just fifteen years old. A forever love. Their forever. <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"...he made my impossible, possible. And he had absolutely no idea he was doing it."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>The second half of the book....watching Cam and Lucy fight for that love.....it hurt. It made me cry. My heart broke for them. There was pain. There was loss. There was heart-ache. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1397190098ra/9244757.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But their love for each other was so strong. Not once did I ever question that love. Despite what Cam and Lucy went through, I never once doubted their devotion to each other. I was never once uncertain about how they felt about each other. <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"I love you, Lucy. I'll always love you, even if you don't know it. So...even if forever is eternal, I promise to love you for our forever."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403535416i/10104865.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Their love story wasn't perfect, but it was theirs. It was their forever. <br><br><b>Emotional...<br>Breathtaking...<br>Heart-Breaking...<br>Inspiring...<br>Hopeful...<br>Beautiful...<br>Forever...</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1390095429ra/8143127.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>ARC kindly provided by the author in exchange for an honest review</i>
</b></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/769362056?book_show_action=true">Nov 19, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer Kyle" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle">Jennifer Kyle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/22555143-more-than-forever">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9916227-jennifer-kyle?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9916227-jennifer-kyle?shelf=book-boyfriends">book-boyfriends</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer769362056" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8648493920798807089">Wow! Just Wow! Lucy and Cameron’s story was wonderful in every way possible. <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405264722i/10373810._SX540_.jpg' width='390' height='480' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Jay McLean finally shared with fans of this series the complete story of Lucy and Cameron. They have been in each book of this series and always inspired the struggling couple that love conquers all. Jay McLean took Lucy our quirky funny character and didn’t overdo her (which I was worried about) and added Cameron who was just completely swoonworthy and most definitely fierce. She told their story one of sadness and hop</span>
  <span id="freeText8648493920798807089" style="display:none">Wow! Just Wow! Lucy and Cameron’s story was wonderful in every way possible. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405264722i/10373810._SX540_.jpg" width="390" height="480" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Jay McLean finally shared with fans of this series the complete story of Lucy and Cameron. They have been in each book of this series and always inspired the struggling couple that love conquers all. Jay McLean took Lucy our quirky funny character and didn’t overdo her (which I was worried about) and added Cameron who was just completely swoonworthy and most definitely fierce. She told their story one of sadness and hope did it with humor, steam and heart.<br><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br>This story is an experience, one of a first love that never diminished through the years. It will have you laughing and crying while you accompany them experiencing all their firsts together. <br><br>Overall, this story is must read for fans of the series, and for those who dream of a love like theirs.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1491900753ra/22458825.gif" width="390" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>”You can keep your two wishes, I’ll just take the one. I want my girl, Lucy. My forever. And not just for our forever, but for eternity, and for always.”</i>
</b><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="8648493920798807089" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1122998150" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1122998150" />
    <a title="Catarina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11538033-catarina"><img alt="Catarina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514808293p2/11538033.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1122998150?book_show_action=true">Dec 04, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer3695281664249189473"> <b>5 Eternal Stars.</b>	<br/><br/>Cameron and Lucy fell in love when they were 15 years old and Lucy’s life was in a bad place. They never stopped falling in love and when they go to college they still are much in love as the first day. <br/>They shared everything: smiles, tears, laughter, the first experiences and their lives. However their story isn’t perfect. It install always unicorn-shaped rainbows and cupcakes. Their story had up’s and downs. Happy and sad tears. Bad moments and amazing ones. <br/>So jump on this a</span>
  <span id="freeText3695281664249189473" style="display:none"> <b>5 Eternal Stars.</b>	<br><br>Cameron and Lucy fell in love when they were 15 years old and Lucy’s life was in a bad place. They never stopped falling in love and when they go to college they still are much in love as the first day. <br>They shared everything: smiles, tears, laughter, the first experiences and their lives. However their story isn’t perfect. It install always unicorn-shaped rainbows and cupcakes. Their story had up’s and downs. Happy and sad tears. Bad moments and amazing ones. <br>So jump on this and read their journey. It surely is an amazing one. <br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418233901i/12718101.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">´<br>I fell in love with Cameron and Lucy in the first book and their story didn’t disappointed. Not only this is probably my new favorite NA book, but it has to be one of the bests ever written. Yes, it had some angst, but we’re dealing with teenagers turning into adults: it was prone to have. For every angsty moment we had an amazing one so it was all good. And the Aladdin stuff was seriously awesome! This was a beautiful story and I loved how it begin when they were 15 and went on the rest of their lives. If you’re looking for an amazing romance book, please, try this one. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1402872274i/10002999.jpg" width="350" height="170" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <b>Rating: </b> 5 Stars. <br> <b>Characters Development: </b> These two broke my heart and sew it back together again in just a few chapters. They’re one of my favorite couples ever written. I loved Lucy since the first book (probably because she’s a Bookaholic and we can totally relate to that :P) and I loved her even more in this book. And Cam? Cameron is the most considerate, sweet and amazing guy. I loved how he always was there for Lucy and even when he was too stupid for his own good (oh well, guys…) he was always too swoony and honest and impossible not to love him. I loved Lucy’s brothers and how the rest of the gang was always there for them. Best group of friends, ever! <br> <b>Steam: </b> Nice hot moments. <br> <b>Sensible Subjects: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br> <b>Love Triangle: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Cheating: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br> <b>HEA: </b>	<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Yes. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_1251660640" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1251660640" />
    <a title="Carol [Goodreads Addict]" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict"><img alt="Carol [Goodreads Addict]" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1551124421p2/10717098.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1251660640?book_show_action=true">Apr 10, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Carol [Goodreads Addict]" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Carol [Goodreads Addict]" href="/user/show/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict">Carol [Goodreads Addict]</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1251660640" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5047421011144570507"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1428525313i/14440048._SX540_.jpg' alt='teacups and book love: Cover Reveal: More Than Forever by Jay ...' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>More Than Forever is book four in the More Than series by Jay McLean. We have grown to know and love Cameron and Lucy in the first three books of this series but we didn’t know their history, how they started. This book takes us back to when they were fifteen years old and first met. I wasn’t sure if I would like going back that far but it took all of about two pages to get me hooked. <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1428889791i/14492359.jpg' alt='more than forever jay mclean - Google Search' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>Lucy is fifteen years old and her mother is dying of cancer. She has six younger brothers, one just a baby. Cam</span>
  <span id="freeText5047421011144570507" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1428525313i/14440048._SX540_.jpg" alt="teacups and book love: Cover Reveal: More Than Forever by Jay ..." class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>More Than Forever is book four in the More Than series by Jay McLean. We have grown to know and love Cameron and Lucy in the first three books of this series but we didn’t know their history, how they started. This book takes us back to when they were fifteen years old and first met. I wasn’t sure if I would like going back that far but it took all of about two pages to get me hooked. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1428889791i/14492359.jpg" alt="more than forever jay mclean - Google Search" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Lucy is fifteen years old and her mother is dying of cancer. She has six younger brothers, one just a baby. Cameron has noticed her at school but they haven’t talked. But then her mother dies, and Cameron saves Lucy.<br><br><b>
  <i>“If heartbreak had a face, hers would be it.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1428889791i/14492360._SX540_.jpg" alt="Couple Sitting Outdoors Stock Photos - Image: 32212573" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Fifteen year old Cameron just starts showing up at Lucy’s house every day. He somehow just knows what to do, how to help put her back together again. The road isn’t easy but he just keeps showing up and being there for her.<br><br><b>
  <i>“He made my impossible, possible. And he had absolutely no idea he was doing it.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1428889791i/14492361.jpg" alt="More Than Forever" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Lucy and Cameron were just kids. Their relationship was a slow progression. The author did a perfect job of dealing with their relationship in the early years. The road wasn’t easy for them. They had Lucy’s grieving, troubled father to deal with, and all of their own insecurities.<br><br><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/13076707_zpspqtifgid.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1423159236ra/13593454.gif" alt=" photo 13076707_zpspqtifgid.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This book takes us through it all, from high school to college to beyond college. We don’t see much of the other characters we have grown to love until the end but the wait is so well worth it. We also meet Cameron’s college roommate, Minge, who I loved. I hope we get to see more of him.<br><br><b>
  <i>"You make my world stop, Lucy."</i>
</b> <br><br>There was so much they had to deal with, things you had no idea were going on when you read the first three books. This is Lucy and Cameron, though. They have been together since they were fifteen. They were strong enough to get through anything, right? <br><br>Again, I have to say that in this book, as I have said in the other books, I love the parents. Cameron’s Mom and her boyfriend are so completely supportive and awesome. And once Lucy’s Dad got himself straightened out he was pretty awesome himself. <br><br>Through it all, I had to keep telling myself that these are kids, they were each other’s firsts for everything. So no matter how perfect they seem, there are going to eventually be problems. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1428889791i/14492362._SX540_.jpg" alt="Gallery For &gt; Sunset Pictures With Couples" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>The ending of this book…sigh…well, it’s wonderful. As I said before, we get plenty of the other couples in the end, and it’s perfect. Every book in this series gets better and better. Jay McLean, as a writer, gets better with each book. I admit that I am addicted to this series. I can’t wait for book five to come out, More Than Enough. This is one of those authors that once you get hooked, you can’t help but to read anything and everything she writes. This is something I plan to continue doing. So if you haven’t started this series yet, if it’s sitting on your reading device and you just haven’t gotten to it, I encourage you to give it a try. I think you will fall in love just as I have.<br><br><b>
  <i>“You’re my art, Luce. My heart.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1425952445ra/13954015.gif" alt="signature" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="5047421011144570507" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jess-i-ca ~Sometimes a Gif Witch~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jess-i-ca ~Sometimes a Gif Witch~" href="/user/show/8740772-jess-i-ca-sometimes-a-gif-witch">Jess-i-ca ~Sometimes a Gif Witch~</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8740772-jess-i-ca-sometimes-a-gif-witch?shelf=this-has-some-funny-shit">this-has-some-funny-shit</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer735015915" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1786396836015819811"><b> 5 - Best of the series - Stars</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"Love has no limits. No boundaries. No time. It's eternal. Forever."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br/>How many people can say they met their soul mate at 15? <br/><br/>For Lucy <i>"Clitorusaurus-rex"</i> Preston <br/><br/><a href='http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY%203/b29c3ed3-43b6-4ce8-adad-f80bcd9fdf4c_zpsc2050408.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403625834i/10120618.jpg' alt=' photo b29c3ed3-43b6-4ce8-adad-f80bcd9fdf4c_zpsc2050408.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>and Cameron Aladdin Gordon <br/><br/><a href='http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY%203/19b44008-9882-45cd-81f9-be2d78d135a3_zps604a5d01.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403625834i/10120619.jpg' alt=' photo 19b44008-9882-45cd-81f9-be2d78d135a3_zps604a5d01.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>they can say it was fate that brought them together at 15. Unfortunately at the time the fate that brought them together was Lucy's mother passing away. <br/><br/><a href='http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY/tumblr_mcztp5ylLb1rum5tfo4_500_zps7f69c3ea.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1391187668ra/8343960.gif' alt='crying photo tumblr_mcztp5ylLb1rum5tfo4_500_zps7f69c3ea.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Cameron stepped in and helped Lucy when she needed it. He became her strength and support. He saved her </span>
  <span id="freeText1786396836015819811" style="display:none"><b> 5 - Best of the series - Stars</b><br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"Love has no limits. No boundaries. No time. It's eternal. Forever."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>How many people can say they met their soul mate at 15? <br><br>For Lucy <i>"Clitorusaurus-rex"</i> Preston <br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY%203/b29c3ed3-43b6-4ce8-adad-f80bcd9fdf4c_zpsc2050408.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403625834i/10120618.jpg" alt=" photo b29c3ed3-43b6-4ce8-adad-f80bcd9fdf4c_zpsc2050408.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>and Cameron Aladdin Gordon <br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY%203/19b44008-9882-45cd-81f9-be2d78d135a3_zps604a5d01.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403625834i/10120619.jpg" alt=" photo 19b44008-9882-45cd-81f9-be2d78d135a3_zps604a5d01.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>they can say it was fate that brought them together at 15. Unfortunately at the time the fate that brought them together was Lucy's mother passing away. <br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY/tumblr_mcztp5ylLb1rum5tfo4_500_zps7f69c3ea.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1391187668ra/8343960.gif" alt="crying photo tumblr_mcztp5ylLb1rum5tfo4_500_zps7f69c3ea.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Cameron stepped in and helped Lucy when she needed it. He became her strength and support. He saved her when she didn't think she needed it. He became a role model for her brothers<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"Because in a time of nothing but pain, and anger, and emptiness, and hurt....he healed me.<br>He made it stop.<br>He made it better.<br>He made me fall in love.<br>Love.<br>I love him."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1403626292ra/10120666.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>They experience many first together as their relationship progresses and often times these experiences were hysterical.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1403626559ra/10120720.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>They are like two peas in a pod, always together and always wanting to be together. It's almost as if they live for each other.<br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY%203/tumblr_mn3zf4iHOp1sp9fcho1_r1_500_zps383656b2.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1400680420ra/9706861.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mn3zf4iHOp1sp9fcho1_r1_500_zps383656b2.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>As they grow up and grow together, life happens and Lucy and Cam have to continuously fight to keep their love strong. They have college, work, new friends and other commitments all before them. What happens when the one person who you always rely on is no longer constantly there? <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"Because he's Cameron. And you're Lucy. You're team Luca. You guys are forever. If you two can't make it work, then we're all screwed."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>They experience many ups and downs, pain and heartbreak and you can't help but root for them and hope they pull through to get their happy ending.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1403625563ra/10120596.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When I finally got to the end I almost felt a Celine Dion would have been appropriate for me and my happy tears, so here you go. <br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://youtu.be/VTxnqUhhlIY">http://youtu.be/VTxnqUhhlIY</a><br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"I want my girl, Lucy. My forever. And not just for our forever, but for eternity, and for always."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY%203/tumblr_n7f8tsaBeq1ry5ojao1_400_zpscf0afada.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1403620610ra/10119696.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_n7f8tsaBeq1ry5ojao1_400_zpscf0afada.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I will admit I was scared the book was going to be mainly drunk Lucy<br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY%203/tumblr_mzmkteDEq51r4ueyro1_500_zpsc0aeefac.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1403620610ra/10119697.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mzmkteDEq51r4ueyro1_500_zpsc0aeefac.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>but luckily that wasn't the case, so Jay<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1403623941ra/10120379.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>
  <u>A few more of my random thoughts and comments</u>
</b><br><br>- There were a few minor things that I didn't care for in the story but I felt the overall story made up for them so that's why i still rated it a 5. <br><br>- Laughed my ass off about the vagina discussion. I tend to agree with Lucy and think they look weird. ;)<br><br>- Also Cameron and Minge with the text acting like One-Directioners -<br> <b>H-I-L-A-R-I-O-U-S!</b><br><br>- Love how the rest of the gang was included throughout the book and how close their group is.<br><br>- Love, <b>Love <u>LOVED</u></b> the Aladdin stuff, especially Cam's story.<br><br>- It was a little more angst than I overall like but bonus for no grey eyes, no running, no Harvard or Yale. <br><br>- If you know me, then you may or may not know my history with the famous Jay McLean, and I'm happy to report this book had <b>Legit count - Only 4</b> <br><br>Anyways, its good and you should read it.<br><br> <a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY%202/tumblr_ly46efb4rN1rn4jhdo1_500_zps6a92750d.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1394677314ra/8888061.gif" alt="thumbs up photo tumblr_ly46efb4rN1rn4jhdo1_500_zps6a92750d.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i>ARC provided by the author for an honest legit review. </i>

<div id="review_1050839521" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1050839521" />
    <a title="Wendy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/32445724-wendy"><img alt="Wendy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1551516258p2/32445724.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1050839521?book_show_action=true">Sep 10, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Wendy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Wendy" href="/user/show/32445724-wendy">Wendy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/32445724-wendy?shelf=college">college</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/32445724-wendy?shelf=will-read-again">will-read-again</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/32445724-wendy?shelf=dirty-talk">dirty-talk</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/32445724-wendy?shelf=sweet">sweet</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/32445724-wendy?shelf=emotional">emotional</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/32445724-wendy?shelf=ya-na">ya-na</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/32445724-wendy?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/32445724-wendy?shelf=laughed-my-ass-off">laughed-my-ass-off</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/32445724-wendy?shelf=now-thats-hot">now-thats-hot</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/32445724-wendy?shelf=i-m-not-crying-you-are-crying">i-m-not-crying-you-are-crying</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1050839521" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7994157501766991728">While I am waiting for some awesome books to be released, I am re-reading some all time favorits of mine. This one is definitely in my "all time" top 5. I have read this book so many times already, yet it never gets old. The reason I am so in love with it, is because it gave me so many feels....<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1437996375ra/15654150.gif' alt='26627_orig.gif (500×283)' width='299' height='169' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>One minute I was laughing my ass off and the next is was crying my eyes out. Laughing, crying, cursing, swooning...I loved every single second of it.<br/><br/>Not only is this book one of my favorite m/f books ever</span>
  <span id="freeText7994157501766991728" style="display:none">While I am waiting for some awesome books to be released, I am re-reading some all time favorits of mine. This one is definitely in my "all time" top 5. I have read this book so many times already, yet it never gets old. The reason I am so in love with it, is because it gave me so many feels....<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1437996375ra/15654150.gif" alt="26627_orig.gif (500×283)" width="299" height="169" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>One minute I was laughing my ass off and the next is was crying my eyes out. Laughing, crying, cursing, swooning...I loved every single second of it.<br><br>Not only is this book one of my favorite m/f books ever...it also has one of my favorite couples in it. These two were the best !! So let me introduce you ;)<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1492011359i/22472824._SX540_.jpg" alt="1794b61eeb94ef7fcd2907bbd931c452.jpg (550×348): " width="382" height="242" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Lucy is just a teenager (15) when her life completely changes, when her mother dies. She is trying her best to keep her family together, but everything is falling apart. She can't do it all by herself and thankfully, she doesn't have to. Because this is when Cameron comes in. Even at 15 years old, this boy stole my freaking heart. He is one of the greatest hero's I have ever read about.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1421876901ra/13424908.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>He is her little brothers baseball coach and he also goes to the same high school. He has seen Lucy aroud and he knows she is struggeling. From the moment he saw her, he knew that she was it for him and he tries his very best to be the rock that she needs...<br><br><em><strong>“I thought it was impossible to be able to laugh again. But he did it; he made my impossible, possible”</strong> </em><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1492011359i/22472825.jpg" alt="ba5f13b9bbf8c55ccdfe04dc65783c5a.jpg (500×515): " width="203" height="209" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It was so beautiful seeing these two falling in love. It was so sweet, but it was also so freaking funny !!!<br><br><strong>
  <em>“I move my hand lower. His eyes drift shut. Lower. He lets out a groan. And then I touch it. "Shit," he breathes. "Penis," I squeak.”</em>
</strong><br><br>I loved that they experienced all their first together !!<br><br>What I also loved about this book was the supporting cast. Cam's mother was amazing, but it was his stepdad Mark that blew me away...what a great man !!!<br><br>These two might have been young when they started their relationship, but they knew exactly what they were feeling and what they wanted. It was awesome watching them grow older and Lucy...damn she was my kind of girl. A book geek with a big mouth !!<br><br><em><strong>“Quit moaning like a dick deprived whore and get out of my seat.”</strong> </em><br><br>But when they get older...things aren't always so easy anymore. They go of to collage and hat's when the troubles start. My heart broke into a million pieces reading about them struggeling. I know Cameron didn't mean to, but he still brok her heart.....and mine. I didn't hate him though...I could never hate him.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492011359ra/22472826.gif" alt="tumblr_n88hmsv3Vk1ts7f01o1_500.gif (500×281)" width="372" height="209" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><em>
  <strong>“And at her words, I release her. Because the last thing I ever wanted was to hurt her.”</strong>
</em><br><br>But....and this is why I love Cam sooooo freaking much....he doesn't give up. He will never give up on Lucy. These two are real soulmates, I don't think one would be able to survive without the other....<br><br><em>
  <strong>“There is a love so fierce it cannot be measured. A heart so strong it will never slow. There is a promise so sure it can never lie. And we promise that love forever. Forever and always”</strong>
</em><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492011359ra/22472827.gif" alt="227378-Silhouette-Kiss.gif (500×266)" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>If I could give this book 10 stars...I would !!!!<br><br><blockquote>

<div id="review_810344536" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/810344536" />
    <a title="Patrycja" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6852653-patrycja"><img alt="Patrycja" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1586460589p2/6852653.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/810344536?book_show_action=true">Jan 03, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Patrycja" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Patrycja" href="/user/show/6852653-patrycja">Patrycja</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer810344536" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2405099068085393979"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391618077i/8420433._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='40' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Title:</b> More Than Forever<br/><b>Series:</b> More #4<br/><b>Author:</b> Jay McLean <br/><b>Release Date: </b> July 2014<br/><b>Rating:</b> 4.5 stars<br/><b>Cliffhanger:</b>. No<br/><b> HEA: </b> <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[ Yes  <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391618077i/8420434._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='40' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>I fell in love with Jay Mclean’s characters last summer. My adoration for them was instant. Seconds after meeting this bunch of funny and sweet teenagers I connected with them. From that point I knew I had to read every story McLean will write about them. <br/><br/>I really adored previous instalments of More series, but after reading about Cam and L</span>
  <span id="freeText2405099068085393979" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391618077i/8420433._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Title:</b> More Than Forever<br><b>Series:</b> More #4<br><b>Author:</b> Jay McLean <br><b>Release Date: </b> July 2014<br><b>Rating:</b> 4.5 stars<br><b>Cliffhanger:</b>. No<br><b> HEA: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Yes  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391618077i/8420434._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>I fell in love with Jay Mclean’s characters last summer. My adoration for them was instant. Seconds after meeting this bunch of funny and sweet teenagers I connected with them. From that point I knew I had to read every story McLean will write about them. <br><br>I really adored previous instalments of More series, but after reading about Cam and Lucy’s breathtaking journey I have to say I’m not only in love with it but in awe with how beautiful it was. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405356456i/10385803._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"Because in a time of nothing but pain, and anger, and emptiness, and hurt....he healed me.<br>He made it stop.<br>He made it better.<br>He made me fall in love.<br>Love.<br>I love him."</i>
</b><br><br><br>With every new book in the More series, I was able to see glimpses of how perfect and how beautiful Cam and Lucy’s relationship was. They always shined brightly and made everything just a little bit better, even though they were only secondary characters. Lucy’s quirkiness and Cam’s giving personality drew me in and made me want to know everything about them.<br> <br>More Than Forever finally gave me the chance to learn absolutely every detail about their love; love they found while being only 15. Although, they relationship seemed to be very easy while I’d seen it through others eyes, the truth is that’s not the case at all. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405356456i/10385804._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Lucy and Cam’s story is full of up and downs; angst and sorrow, happiness and pain. It’s a story about finding your soul mate and constantly fighting for it to stay that way. <br><br>There is so many wonderful things I loved in this story. The witty banter, laugh out loud moments, beautiful heart-to-heart conversations, irresistible characters and fabulous connection between two main heroes made More Than Forever beautiful read. It grabbed a hold of my heart and didn’t let go till I turned off my ereader. It was heart wrenching story about finding your ‘forever person’ at only 15 and I loved every second of it. <br><br><b>
  <i>”You can keep your two wishes, I’ll just take the one. I want my girl, Lucy. My forever. And not just for our forever, but for eternity, and for always.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405356456i/10385805.jpg" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>FOLLOW SMOKIN
