<div id="review_845083612" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/845083612" />
    <a title="* Meli Mel *" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10905711-meli-mel"><img alt="* Meli Mel *" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577750127p2/10905711.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/845083612?book_show_action=true">Feb 04, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="* Meli Mel *" class="user" itemprop="url" name="* Meli Mel *" href="/user/show/10905711-meli-mel">* Meli Mel *</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/22555143-more-than-forever">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=broken-heroine">broken-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=dual-pov">dual-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=drama-rama-bo-bama">drama-rama-bo-bama</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=virgin-heroine">virgin-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=heart-breaking">heart-breaking</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=fav-book-boyfriend">fav-book-boyfriend</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=hells-yeah-alphas">hells-yeah-alphas</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=super-steamy">super-steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10905711-meli-mel?shelf=uber-sweet">uber-sweet</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer845083612" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1873498754267442477"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401972i/780787._SX540_.jpg' width='125' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>♥♥♥ 5 "I Want Cameron" Stars ♥♥♥</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1405915447ra/10470899.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ●<br/><br/>“You make my world stop, Lucy.”<br/><br/>● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ●</b>
</blockquote><br/>I have been wanting to read this book since the moment I found out that it was going to exist. Cam and Lucy were one of my favourite couples of the series. And after seeing them a few times in the previous books, I wanted to know how they came to be. I was a bit worried that their book wouldn't end up being good for me and that I would get disappointed. But, th</span>
  <span id="freeText1873498754267442477" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401972i/780787._SX540_.jpg" width="125" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>♥♥♥ 5 "I Want Cameron" Stars ♥♥♥</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1405915447ra/10470899.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ●<br><br>“You make my world stop, Lucy.”<br><br>● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ●</b>
</blockquote><br>I have been wanting to read this book since the moment I found out that it was going to exist. Cam and Lucy were one of my favourite couples of the series. And after seeing them a few times in the previous books, I wanted to know how they came to be. I was a bit worried that their book wouldn't end up being good for me and that I would get disappointed. But, that was not the case. At. All. I freaking loved this book. It's probably my favourite of the series.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403727639i/10136566._SX540_.png" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I actually loved the way this book was written. It starts off by showing the reader how Lucy and Cam met, which wasn't during the best of circumstances. I had no idea how much pain and heartbreak these two had gone through. What I thought was going to be a light read, became so much more.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405914531i/10470770._SY540_.png" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I loved Lucy! But, I had no idea all that she went through after her mother passed away. It was painful to read. She had no one until Cam came into the picture. I loved seeing her slowly become stronger. It was so wonderful to see him support her and take care of her. Lucy was great, quite mature for her age. Once she came out of her shell, I loved how funny she could be, especially when she was drunk. I loved her book nerd ways and the weird funny random comments that came out of her mouth.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ●<br><br>“It’s the sunrise and sunset. He says it reminds him of our love. Because it’s eternal- the rise and fall of the sun. It’s forever. Just like us.”<br><br>● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ●</b>
</blockquote><br>I absolutely LOVED Cam!! He is the most amazing and perfect boyfriend ever!! I seriously want him for myself. He was just so kind and caring when it came to Lucy and her younger brothers. He made me melt so many times with his sweetness. But I also loved when he became all alpha and jealous of anyone who looked interested in Lucy. It was just awesome. I loved seeing how he was raised and I loved both his parents. Mark was the best, even if he wasn't Cam's real father, I loved how much he cared for Cam and how he was always there for him.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405914531i/10470771._SY540_.png" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>What I really enjoyed was all the antics in this book. It was freaking hilarious!! I loved seeing all the other characters from the previous books in this one. You just have no idea how much I laughed at all of the stuff that happened and the hilarious banter. Which I was grateful for, because there were a lot of sad parts that had me crying my eyes out. I really loved the fact that even though Lucy and Cam's story intertwined with the other characters, she didn't go over it in detail. I mean we already know what happens from reading their book. So, I was glad she made this completely Cam and Lucy's story.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ●<br><br>“There is a love so fierce it cannot be measured. <br>A heart so strong it will never slow. <br>There is a promise so sure it can never lie. <br>And we promise that love forever. <br>Forever and always” <br><br>● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ●</b>
</blockquote><br>Their journey to their HEA, was a long and heartbreaking one. But, it was also really beautiful. I felt a lot of different emotions. I smiled, fell in love, relived first times, and cried so hard. But, I loved it all despite the hurt. They had so many ups and downs throughout their years together, but their love only got stronger. I loved it! The ending and epilogue were beautiful. Like I mentioned before, this is now my favourite of the series. I just can't stop saying how much I truly loved this book. So, you are just going to have to read it for yourself. Now, I can't wait to read he next!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403727639i/10136566._SX540_.png" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="1873498754267442477" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5494655-brandi?shelf=all-time-favorites">all-time-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5494655-brandi?shelf=emotional">emotional</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5494655-brandi?shelf=2014-favorite">2014-favorite</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer769873811" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4221834065006705924"><b> 5 stars </b><br/> <br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405515904i/10408393._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>"You still make my world stop, Luce."</i>
</b><br/><br/>Cam and Lucy's story was everything I wished for. It was beautiful, heartbreaking and hopeful. When Lucy's mother passes, she is struggling to hold on, helping care for her brothers and dealing with her own grief. Enter Cameron. Seriously, this guy is PERFECTION. He is determined to help Lucy.<br/><br/><i>
  <b>"Because while she's so pre-occupied reading... I'm so pre-occupied reading her."</b>
</i><br/><br/>Experiencing the beginning of their love story was amazing. They were </span>
  <span id="freeText4221834065006705924" style="display:none"><b> 5 stars </b><br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405515904i/10408393._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"You still make my world stop, Luce."</i>
</b><br><br>Cam and Lucy's story was everything I wished for. It was beautiful, heartbreaking and hopeful. When Lucy's mother passes, she is struggling to hold on, helping care for her brothers and dealing with her own grief. Enter Cameron. Seriously, this guy is PERFECTION. He is determined to help Lucy.<br><br><i>
  <b>"Because while she's so pre-occupied reading... I'm so pre-occupied reading her."</b>
</i><br><br>Experiencing the beginning of their love story was amazing. They were so adorable, I loved everything minute.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405515904i/10408394._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="380" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But as time passes, they face new challenges, life is not as easy as it once was. Watching them struggle, broke my heart. The pain and the loss that they experience. It hurt.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/558750.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Through everything, their devotion to each other never wavered. They struggled, yes. But their love for each other always shined through. I absolutely adore this series and highly recommend it to everyone!<br><br><b>
  <i>"Love has no limits. No boundaries. No time. It's eternal. Forever."</i>
</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="4221834065006705924" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_739751755" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/739751755" />
    <a title="Seena Seena " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2875657-seena-seena"><img alt="Seena Seena " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1304423151p2/2875657.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/739751755?book_show_action=true">Oct 12, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Seena Seena " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Seena Seena " href="/user/show/2875657-seena-seena">Seena Seena </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2875657-seena-seena?shelf=my-fav-s">my-fav-s</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer739751755" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5337930186171750401">My review will be a jumble of thoughts because I only just finished the book and all my emotions are running inside my head!<br/><br/>Firstly, Jay McLean once again has delivered a book so perfect, enough silly, enough smiles, enough laughs, enough drama and most of all enough love. <br/><br/><a href='http://s945.photobucket.com/user/Mersina84/media/tumblr_inline_mz2m4s8I3e1s2e3mn_zpse0efce43.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396263657ra/9107827.gif' alt=' photo tumblr_inline_mz2m4s8I3e1s2e3mn_zpse0efce43.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Before you even open this book, you MUST read the previous 3 titles in the series:<br/><br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18285151.More_Than_This__More___1_' title='More Than This (More, #1) by Jay McLean' rel='nofollow noopener'>More Than This</a><br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18215175.More_Than_Her__More___2_' title='More Than Her (More, #2) by Jay McLean' rel='nofollow noopener'>More Than Her</a><br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18879990.More_Than_Him__More___3_' title='More Than Him (More, #3) by Jay McLean' rel='nofollow noopener'>More Than Him</a><br/><br/>And seriously if you haven't already read these books?<br/><br/><a href='http://s945.photobucket.com/user/Mersina84/media/tumblr_inline_mq3hg8WXS41qz4rgp_zps9a539c3c.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396263657ra/9107823.gif' alt=' photo tumblr_inline_mq3hg8WXS41qz4rgp_zps9a539c3c.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Anyway, back to the story....<br/><br/>We start off </span>
  <span id="freeText5337930186171750401" style="display:none">My review will be a jumble of thoughts because I only just finished the book and all my emotions are running inside my head!<br><br>Firstly, Jay McLean once again has delivered a book so perfect, enough silly, enough smiles, enough laughs, enough drama and most of all enough love. <br><br><a href="http://s945.photobucket.com/user/Mersina84/media/tumblr_inline_mz2m4s8I3e1s2e3mn_zpse0efce43.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396263657ra/9107827.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_inline_mz2m4s8I3e1s2e3mn_zpse0efce43.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Before you even open this book, you MUST read the previous 3 titles in the series:<br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18285151.More_Than_This__More___1_" title="More Than This (More, #1) by Jay McLean" rel="nofollow noopener">More Than This</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18215175.More_Than_Her__More___2_" title="More Than Her (More, #2) by Jay McLean" rel="nofollow noopener">More Than Her</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18879990.More_Than_Him__More___3_" title="More Than Him (More, #3) by Jay McLean" rel="nofollow noopener">More Than Him</a><br><br>And seriously if you haven't already read these books?<br><br><a href="http://s945.photobucket.com/user/Mersina84/media/tumblr_inline_mq3hg8WXS41qz4rgp_zps9a539c3c.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396263657ra/9107823.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_inline_mq3hg8WXS41qz4rgp_zps9a539c3c.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Anyway, back to the story....<br><br>We start off when Lucy was only the wee little age of 15.<br>And the first few chapters of this book absolutely broke me! I have not emotionally gut wrenching sobbed cried because of a book in so long.<br><br><a href="http://s945.photobucket.com/user/Mersina84/media/tumblr_inline_mviisrNQcB1rrhd9i_zps08062455.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1405159465ra/10353781.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_inline_mviisrNQcB1rrhd9i_zps08062455.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The first few chapters hit to close to home for me, but McLean does it justice and has so beautifully written a very hard emotion. But McLean you broke me for a little while there!!<br><br><a href="http://s945.photobucket.com/user/Mersina84/media/tumblr_mbdvtac2oH1rvywo4_zps608281df.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1405159465ra/10353783.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mbdvtac2oH1rvywo4_zps608281df.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>But it was all worth it, because as Cam mended our Lucy together, I felt as though he mended me in the process.<br><br><a href="http://s945.photobucket.com/user/Mersina84/media/tumblr_mmfg18CNwY1ry4q0lo1_500_zpse10f0683.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1405159465ra/10353784.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mmfg18CNwY1ry4q0lo1_500_zpse10f0683.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And Cam, my god there are no words I can use to express the sheer fabulosity that is Cam! When he steps up and faces Lucy's father for her, I absolutely melted for him.<br><br><a href="http://s945.photobucket.com/user/Mersina84/media/tumblr_inline_mg4nwkFyjR1ry4qim_zps3fbea94d.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1405159465ra/10353785.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_inline_mg4nwkFyjR1ry4qim_zps3fbea94d.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>That line he says when Lucy laughs for the first time after her mother dies, <b>"You make my world stop, Lucy."</b> that moment and those emotions, my god! <br><br><a href="http://s945.photobucket.com/user/Mersina84/media/tumblr_inline_mxknh7HoJW1rbumi6_zps55eac1a3.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1405159465ra/10353786.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_inline_mxknh7HoJW1rbumi6_zps55eac1a3.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And the feelings! It's a crazy roller coaster ride!<br>I don't drink but I felt like a needed a drink on more than one occasion!<br><br><a href="http://s945.photobucket.com/user/Mersina84/media/tumblr_inline_mvlicwd3tY1s2m7xu_zpsbff7a024.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1405159465ra/10353787.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_inline_mvlicwd3tY1s2m7xu_zpsbff7a024.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Even though you know going in that they had love from the start, it was not an easy ride for them.<br><br>At first loss and heartache!<br><br><a href="http://s945.photobucket.com/user/Mersina84/media/tumblr_mq6gdnHdto1sqq4f7o1_500_zps37b205fd.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1405159465ra/10353788.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mq6gdnHdto1sqq4f7o1_500_zps37b205fd.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Then the firsts!<br><br><a href="http://s945.photobucket.com/user/Mersina84/media/tumblr_mcn2d6HuFy1rp8ohq_zps5b2328cb.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1405159465ra/10353789.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mcn2d6HuFy1rp8ohq_zps5b2328cb.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And then the funnies!<br><br><a href="http://s945.photobucket.com/user/Mersina84/media/tumblr_mtfvqyDFLr1reyksgo1_500_zpsfc1b8fcd.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396263657ra/9107830.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mtfvqyDFLr1reyksgo1_500_zpsfc1b8fcd.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And then the insecurities!<br><br><a href="http://s945.photobucket.com/user/Mersina84/media/tumblr_mq6gn1vtSm1sqq4f7o1_500_zps685b1c72.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1405159466ra/10353790.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mq6gn1vtSm1sqq4f7o1_500_zps685b1c72.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And then a certain picture was drawn and I have never felt so much betrayal while reading a book! I was so emotionally upset, that I had to stop!<br><br><a href="http://s945.photobucket.com/user/Mersina84/media/tumblr_inline_mz2lnhHlfU1s2e3mn_zps9a50f1c8.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396263657ra/9107826.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_inline_mz2lnhHlfU1s2e3mn_zps9a50f1c8.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s945.photobucket.com/user/Mersina84/media/tumblr_mvw4ozLKAY1svceedo1_500_zps77b4c80f.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1396263657ra/9107829.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mvw4ozLKAY1svceedo1_500_zps77b4c80f.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And then the hurtful words were said!<br><br><a href="http://s945.photobucket.com/user/Mersina84/media/tumblr_maiyhvNrQh1rakpcyo1_500_zpsf4311c4d.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1405159466ra/10353791.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_maiyhvNrQh1rakpcyo1_500_zpsf4311c4d.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And then the most saddest, heart wrenching heartbreak ever!<br><br><a href="http://s945.photobucket.com/user/Mersina84/media/tumblr_n2lwpyLzBk1tw1vhco1_250_zpsa0702c07.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1405159466ra/10353792.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_n2lwpyLzBk1tw1vhco1_250_zpsa0702c07.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And that stupid no good for nothing Roxy!<br>Hands down, McLean can make you hate a character so much that I actually hate the name Roxy now! That thing needed to be bitch slapped!<br><br><a href="http://s945.photobucket.com/user/Mersina84/media/tumblr_md0sn8UTwx1r1mtsdo2_250_zps600f7988.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1405159466ra/10353793.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_md0sn8UTwx1r1mtsdo2_250_zps600f7988.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>She was just a total Bitch and heartless cow!<br><br><a href="http://s945.photobucket.com/user/Mersina84/media/tumblr_mfgknoLzrk1rxdhmzo4_r1_250_zps9c0c6151.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380397029ra/765709.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mfgknoLzrk1rxdhmzo4_r1_250_zps9c0c6151.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s945.photobucket.com/user/Mersina84/media/tumblr_m953q0Dkz61r7v658_zpsd3ad2053.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1405159466ra/10353794.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_m953q0Dkz61r7v658_zpsd3ad2053.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>But bitch Roxy got her due and it was CLASSIC!<br><br><a href="http://s945.photobucket.com/user/Mersina84/media/tumblr_mfgknoLzrk1rxdhmzo3_250_zpsf153ebed.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380405928ra/791405.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mfgknoLzrk1rxdhmzo3_250_zpsf153ebed.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>So much does happen, you do feel so much and at the end you are left feeling so happy, so lovey dovey and so much HAPPINESS!<br><br><a href="http://s945.photobucket.com/user/Mersina84/media/tumblr_mavzleEVCY1rt8iws_zps886f14ef.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380393549ra/757686.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mavzleEVCY1rt8iws_zps886f14ef.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>AND then your heart stops. Because you realize that you now have to wait for the next book. Like a years wait!<br><br><a href="http://s945.photobucket.com/user/Mersina84/media/tumblr_mamn5n4XYL1qefl5u_zps83802dc7.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380393549ra/757692.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mamn5n4XYL1qefl5u_zps83802dc7.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>But McLean will give us some new goodness in the coming months to tide us over until our next installment of the #MORE series.<br><br><a href="http://s945.photobucket.com/user/Mersina84/media/tumblr_m3bzc40g2o1r1awtfo1_250_zpsf800ce4c.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380393549ra/757687.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_m3bzc40g2o1r1awtfo1_250_zpsf800ce4c.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>So in conclusion to my emotional roller coaster of emotions listed above, just go and read the series PEOPLE!<br><br><a href="http://s945.photobucket.com/user/Mersina84/media/tumblr_luu4btKCsY1r1xhsz_zps9722ed07.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380422139ra/839533.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_luu4btKCsY1r1xhsz_zps9722ed07.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="5337930186171750401" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <a title="Geri Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11757728-geri-reads"><img alt="Geri Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1487874758p2/11757728.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/812695429?book_show_action=true">Jan 05, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Geri Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Geri Reads" href="/user/show/11757728-geri-reads">Geri Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer812695429" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13733635151600407516"><i>5 Cam and Lucy stars!</i><br/><br/>Every since I’ve read More Than This, I wanted to know more about Cam and Lucy. They were the quintessential high school sweetheart. They’ve been together forever and stayed solid even when those around them fell apart. Which is also why I was nervous starting this book because no relationship is that perfect, right? And really, what if Jay McLean would ruin their story for me…forever? <br/><br/>Pfft!<br/><br/>Turns out, my fears were utterly unfounded. Not only is their story perfect, their lo</span>
  <span id="freeText13733635151600407516" style="display:none"><i>5 Cam and Lucy stars!</i><br /><br />Every since I’ve read More Than This, I wanted to know more about Cam and Lucy. They were the quintessential high school sweetheart. They’ve been together forever and stayed solid even when those around them fell apart. Which is also why I was nervous starting this book because no relationship is that perfect, right? And really, what if Jay McLean would ruin their story for me…forever? <br /><br />Pfft!<br /><br />Turns out, my fears were utterly unfounded. Not only is their story perfect, their love for each other is even more breathtaking than I could ever imagine. This book gave me everything; love, angst, jealousy, humor—oh, God, the humor—and then some. I was utterly captivated by Cam and Lucy together. <br /><br /><b>Cameron</b><br /><br /><b>
  <blockquote>Cameron is an artist. He’s an athlete. He’s an unbelievably respectful son. Above all that, Cameron has a heart the size of the ocean.</blockquote>
</b><br /><br />That sums up Cam perfectly. He is just awesome. He’s one of those guys that will make you believe that nice guys do finish first. He’s entirely sweet and funny, and most of all he’s just an all around good person. Cam is AMAZING. <br /><br /><b>Lucy</b><br /><br /><b>
  <blockquote>If heartbreak had a face, hers would be it.</blockquote>
</b><br /> <br />I love Lucy. She's funny but there's an underlying sadness in her character that I found endearing. She carried the entire world in her shoulders when her mom died. She was forced to grow up very fast. She was utterly alone until Cam. <br /><br /><b>
  <blockquote>"...he made my impossible, possible. And he had absolutely no idea he was doing it."</blockquote>
</b><br /><br />The first half of the book takes the reader back to that moment when Cam and Lucy first met. It was a heartbreaking time for Lucy who just lost her mother to cancer. A 15-year old girl suddenly left alone with a big responsibility of taking care of her younger brothers after her own father suffered a breakdown of sorts. <br /><br /><b>
  <blockquote>"You're my art, Luce. My heart."</blockquote>
</b><br /><br />But Cam was there for Lucy and her brothers. He became Lucy’s best friend, confidant and later on, her first and only love. Watching them fall in love was just amazingly sweet. I loved how they were each other firsts and I loved even more the way their family’s reacted to them together. Some of the most hilarious parts of the book involved Cam and Mark (His mom’s partner) having that awkward “talk”. I also enjoyed seeing Lucy and her family especially her brothers.<br /><br /><b>
  <blockquote>“It’s the sunrise and sunset. He says it reminds him of our love. Because it’s eternal- the rise and fall of the sun. It’s forever. Just like us.”</blockquote>
</b><br /><br />The second half was a little more difficult. It was full of angst. Some of the things that happened to Cam and Lucy broke my heart. They knew they were going to be forever. They know they love each other very much but sometimes life happens. They had to go through some rough periods in their relationship. It hurts to read about them but the end result was even better. They certainly did come out of better people and stronger together.<br /><br />I thought Logan and Amanda was my favorite in the series. Turns out, I was wrong. Cam and Lucy’s story owned me. This is, without a doubt, my favorite in the series.<br /> <br /><i>An ARC was provided by Jay McLean in exchange for an honest review.</i></span>

<div id="review_1002914205" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1002914205" />
    <a title="Beverly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13095060-beverly"><img alt="Beverly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1466964369p2/13095060.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1002914205?book_show_action=true">Jul 21, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Beverly" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Beverly" href="/user/show/13095060-beverly">Beverly</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/22555143-more-than-forever">review of another edition</a>


          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Beverly by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle">Jennifer Kyle</a>
  </div>


    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1002914205" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15084255666572962273">One of my favorite things about Jay McLean’s books: her characters love for reading and her reading references. It just makes her books that much more fun. <br/><br/><b>
  <i>"Luce!"<br/><br/>"Is your sister...uh...hearing impaired?"<br/><br/>"No, she's just reading.” </i>
</b><br/><br/><b>5 <i>Luca</i> Stars</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417876041i/12577524._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Like most of my reading buddies, I do not go anywhere without access to my Kindle account. If someone gives me more than a minute I am going to be pulling my book out to read even just a page or two. I picked up reading again after college as a distracti</span>
  <span id="freeText15084255666572962273" style="display:none">One of my favorite things about Jay McLean’s books: her characters love for reading and her reading references. It just makes her books that much more fun. <br><br><b>
  <i>"Luce!"<br><br>"Is your sister...uh...hearing impaired?"<br><br>"No, she's just reading.” </i>
</b><br><br><b>5 <i>Luca</i> Stars</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417876041i/12577524._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Like most of my reading buddies, I do not go anywhere without access to my Kindle account. If someone gives me more than a minute I am going to be pulling my book out to read even just a page or two. I picked up reading again after college as a distraction and became addicted again. Lucy reads for the same reason: distraction. Her mother is dying and she is eldest child and only girl in a family of seven children. <br><br>Lucy is my favorite female character in this series for many reasons: A. We share the same love of books, B. She is so freaking funny, C. She loves with all her heart and takes care of everyone else. D. Did I mention drunk Lucy is a sarcastic bitch? So yes, I love Lucy. <br><br><b>
  <i>"The whore and the pindick. Isn’t that like throwing a hotdog down a hallway?" </i>
</b><br><br>Lucy and Cameron met in high school, while they attended school together they didn’t really notice each other until he saw her at her little brothers' little league game he was coaching. Cam was immediately drawn to the girl who was seemed like she was in her own world, oblivious to things going on around her. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417876041i/12577525._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When Lucy’s mother passes away Cam sees Lucy struggling, barely holding it together and decidest to help. You see when Lucy’s mom died her dad was overcome with grief and checked out on the family. While he wwas present he mostly drank and left Lucy with the burden of caring for them. Cam takes it upon himself to step up and help her. Through this they build a friendship that eventually turns into love.<br><br><b>
  <i>"Sometimes I think that this - you and me - this could be as good as it gets for the rest of my life and that would be perfect. Do you think that is normal? To feel that? To be sixteen and feel like your life begins and ends with one person?”</i>
</b><br><br>While we have known Lucy and Cam throughout the series, this story is told from when they were in high school and goes through college. I loved seeing a young Lucy and Cam. I loved seeing their connection and how much Cam loved Lucy and wanted to take care of her. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417876041i/12577526._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Their connection and story is pretty picture perfect, but things begin getting more difficult as they grow up. They are in college, pursing different careers, working different schedules and real life begins to get in the way. I will be honest seeing Cam and Luce experience real life really broke my heart. I know we have to have conflict to have a book and I know that it wouldn't be very realistic for things to continue on perfectly, but damn. <br><br>Lucy and Cam are not perfect people, they are just two people who decided a long time ago to love each other forever. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417876041i/12577527._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>In the end, I absolutely loved this one. I wish somethings had been different, but I have to give credit where it is due. This book/series has completely pulled me in. I am a huge fan of Jay McLean and highly recommend this one. <br><br><b>
  <i>"Love has no limits. no boundaries. No time. It’s eternal. Forever.”</i>
</b><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="15084255666572962273" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer17208511438929501200"><b>5 stars</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1274.photobucket.com/user/RReadoholic/media/Mobile%20Uploads/20140701_132233-kdcollage_zpsetvs4jyo.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/><br/>With the stress of looking after 6 brothers, Lucy finds a little hope in Cameron. Cameron promised her forever, but will their forever be possible?<br/><br/>When Ive highlighted half the book I know Ive got myself a winner. This book has everything I love: the <b>first love tingles</b>, Cam the<b> sweetheart,</b> Lucy the <b>awesome heroine</b>, the<b> laughs</b>, the<b> angst, </b>the <b>heartbreak, </b>the<b> fun banter </b>with the group,<b> Logan, great family, Mark, </b>the<b> fast paced</b> story, I could go on.<br/><br/>Granted I would have liked a little mor</span>
  <span id="freeText17208511438929501200" style="display:none"><b>5 stars</b><br><br><a href="http://s1274.photobucket.com/user/RReadoholic/media/Mobile%20Uploads/20140701_132233-kdcollage_zpsetvs4jyo.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1404221254i/10209458._SY540_.jpg" width="388" alt=" photo 20140701_132233-kdcollage_zpsetvs4jyo.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>With the stress of looking after 6 brothers, Lucy finds a little hope in Cameron. Cameron promised her forever, but will their forever be possible?<br><br>When Ive highlighted half the book I know Ive got myself a winner. This book has everything I love: the <b>first love tingles</b>, Cam the<b> sweetheart,</b> Lucy the <b>awesome heroine</b>, the<b> laughs</b>, the<b> angst, </b>the <b>heartbreak, </b>the<b> fun banter </b>with the group,<b> Logan, great family, Mark, </b>the<b> fast paced</b> story, I could go on.<br><br>Granted I would have liked a little more Logan and maybe a little more sexy time, also 50-70% had me really worried. But all those small issues didnt matter to me because <b>the romance</b> between these two were adorable and heart clenching. My fav couple of the series.<br><br><b>ARC provided by the Author</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="17208511438929501200" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer768938803" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12533590641356021782">*****A PERFECT TEN*****<br/>(BR with Dee)<br/><br/><a href='http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/b0df31c1688fac37ba540cfb3c17d5c2_zps8c5c087f.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1407050294i/10633763._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo b0df31c1688fac37ba540cfb3c17d5c2_zps8c5c087f.jpg' width='365' height='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/>Every once in a while, there is a book that comes along, that validates my love of reading!<br/><b>"More Than Forever"</b> was one of those books!<br/>This book was <b>PERFECT</b>!!!<br/>It had me laughing out loud so many times.<br/>Then there were times I needed a cold shower, and then tears were shed.<br/>I almost felt like I was in despair during the periods of gut wrenching angst.<br/>Through it all, there were many moments of swooning over Cam!!<br/><br/><br/><a href='http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/e5837b60a35613993caed977b60de0ef_zps53a4cafe.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1407050294i/10633764._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo e5837b60a35613993caed977b60de0ef_zps53a4cafe.jpg' width='365' height='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/>Cam and Lucy are both fifteen and attend the </span>
  <span id="freeText12533590641356021782" style="display:none">*****A PERFECT TEN*****<br>(BR with Dee)<br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/b0df31c1688fac37ba540cfb3c17d5c2_zps8c5c087f.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1407050294i/10633763._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo b0df31c1688fac37ba540cfb3c17d5c2_zps8c5c087f.jpg" width="365" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Every once in a while, there is a book that comes along, that validates my love of reading!<br><b>"More Than Forever"</b> was one of those books!<br>This book was <b>PERFECT</b>!!!<br>It had me laughing out loud so many times.<br>Then there were times I needed a cold shower, and then tears were shed.<br>I almost felt like I was in despair during the periods of gut wrenching angst.<br>Through it all, there were many moments of swooning over Cam!!<br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/e5837b60a35613993caed977b60de0ef_zps53a4cafe.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1407050294i/10633764._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo e5837b60a35613993caed977b60de0ef_zps53a4cafe.jpg" width="365" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Cam and Lucy are both fifteen and attend the same high school when they meet. Lucy has just lost her mother to cancer and is deeply depressed and is forced to act as the caregiver to her six younger brothers since her dad is so devastated by her mom's death, that he mentally checks out for a bit.<br>Cam is instantly drawn to her and just starts showing up at her house. He offers to help her with watching over her brothers.<br>At first she is resistant but soon she gives in to Cam.<br>He helps her to get through the pain and gives her the feeling of hope.<br><br><br><br>Lucy soon becomes attracted to Cam.<br>Their relationship is so sweet and innocent in the beginning. <br>I laughed and sighed at their first kiss and first time getting to second base!! <br>OMG when Cam turns to Mark for advice, I laughed so hard I almost fell off the couch.<br>I loved Mark and his sense of humor, and just how much he truly loved Cam as if he were his own son!!<br><br><br>Soon the two are realizing that they are falling in love with each other, and I felt all the tingly butterflies in the stomach when they first say those three words.<br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/b9d61c37ae53ee8e3c20dd67703ce076_zps14041f8b.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1407050294i/10633765._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo b9d61c37ae53ee8e3c20dd67703ce076_zps14041f8b.jpg" width="365" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>The sexy times were incredibly hot, and I have to mention that they did wait almost two years before they took their relationship to that next level.<br>There were some pretty steamy moments which also ended up being some of the funniest and mortifying moments as well!!<br><br><br><br>Cam was so amazing!!!<br>I have a new book boyfriend added to my top ten.<br>In fact he's going in the top five category!!!<br>There were so many times he did things that made me swoon hard!!<br> <br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/cf3d6f4eb2f2efd0c88867f9ed2cf30b_zps783732ac.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1407050294i/10633766._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo cf3d6f4eb2f2efd0c88867f9ed2cf30b_zps783732ac.jpg" width="365" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>Cam and Lucy's relationship will be tested by several circumstances during their four years at college.<br>I cried for Lucy and felt my heart breaking as if it was all happening to me. That is how good this author tells a story!!<br>I was texting Jen to ask how long the pain goes on for!<br>The angst was just about unbearable for what felt like forever!<br><br><br>But I loved that epilogue!!<br><br>I really can't even express into words just how much I loved this book and how it has made me a HUGE fan of Jay McLean!<br>I haven't read the previous three books but now I'm definitely making it my #1 priority to get to them SOON!!<br><br>If you haven't read this one yet, you should definitely pick it up!!!<br><br>Jen, thank you for pushing me to read this one!!<br>LOVE YOU BABES!!!!!<br></span>

<div id="review_878154731" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/878154731" />
    <a title="Tahsin" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6152472-tahsin"><img alt="Tahsin" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1603245361p2/6152472.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/878154731?book_show_action=true">Mar 10, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tahsin" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tahsin" href="/user/show/6152472-tahsin">Tahsin</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/22711327-more-than-forever">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6152472-tahsin?shelf=billion-stars">billion-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6152472-tahsin?shelf=favourite">favourite</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6152472-tahsin?shelf=good-guy-good-for-her">good-guy-good-for-her</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6152472-tahsin?shelf=really-sweet">really-sweet</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6152472-tahsin?shelf=some-really-sad-shit">some-really-sad-shit</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6152472-tahsin?shelf=twisted-to-perfection">twisted-to-perfection</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6152472-tahsin?shelf=hilarious">hilarious</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6152472-tahsin?shelf=companion-spinoff">companion-spinoff</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6152472-tahsin?shelf=made-me-cry">made-me-cry</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6152472-tahsin?shelf=all-consuming">all-consuming</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer878154731" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10099284299206380767">January 18, 2020<br/>I generally don’t like rereading books I had strong reactions to the first time around because I’m weary I’ll feel the exact same way again. But 5.5 years later, here I am rereading one of my top favourite stories of all time, EVER. The first half is still what dreams are made of, and the second half is still heartwrenchingly realistic. Idk if I’m remembering wrong, or if I’m borrowing elements from the Preston Brothers’ series but I remember there being more to LuCa. No?<br/><br/><br/><b><em>"There a</em></b></span>
  <span id="freeText10099284299206380767" style="display:none">January 18, 2020<br>I generally don’t like rereading books I had strong reactions to the first time around because I’m weary I’ll feel the exact same way again. But 5.5 years later, here I am rereading one of my top favourite stories of all time, EVER. The first half is still what dreams are made of, and the second half is still heartwrenchingly realistic. Idk if I’m remembering wrong, or if I’m borrowing elements from the Preston Brothers’ series but I remember there being more to LuCa. No?<br><br><br><b><em>"There aren't enough stars in the universe to give to this book" </em>stars</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1397474399ra/9280238.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Happy tears though<br><br>I kind of don't know what to do with my self/life now that I've finished this book. Everything just seems so pointless after having my sphere of reference/safety/everything tilted off its axis. This is the kind of book that leaves you in a rut after reading, and I'm definitely there right now. <br><br>The first half of the book is the past. It's from when they first meet and most of their high-school years. It was the sweetest, nicest, the mostfuckingamazing thing I've read in a longassmofo time.<br><br>This was pretty much me the entire first half:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1391627605ra/8422254.gif" width="350" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/637158.gif" width="400" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/521857.gif" width="400" height="225" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1405209673ra/10362111.gif" width="200" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I am not lying when I say I had to get up and pee in the middle of the night while I was reading this, because otherwise I'd have pissed all over my bed. I was crying, and then I was laughing and then I was doing both at once.<br><br>And then the dreaded second half comes along. I was terrified to continue, because nothing good lasts forever. Jay Mclean eased us into it, rather than throw in the reader headfirst in a pile of horseshit. <br><br>Even though the shit that was happening was fucked up, the character from whose POV that was written somehow justified it all for me. Dramatic irony at its finest right here people.<br><br>So of course, I was bawling my eyes out again.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/317548.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386324387ra/7338409.gif" width="350" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386798607ra/7446172.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Cam had me swooning, pretty much the entire time. He's not an asshole - not intentionally, at least; he was the good guy from the very beginning. He didn't have to try to make fall for him; I was a goner from the prologue. <br><br>Lucy, Lucy, Lucy<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1405209673ra/10362112.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>My Lucy in the Sky with Diamonds. (No she's not named after the song, but I have the song stuck in my head right now) She's my main bitch. My #1 Girl. I fucking love her to pieces. She can do no wrong. I am absolutely a million percent biased when it comes to her, because she is fucking real to me. She's the kind of girl that you would encounter in real life, and the fact that she has such an amazing lovestory is what makes me love her.<br><br>You know what the best part of reading this book was? I could see this happen in real life. Every aspect was just so terrifyingly real that it gives the commonfolk, the hopeless romantic, the cynic all believe in love. Cam and Lucy are one of my favorite couples of all time, and I can see them making it through to the other end if this were to be reality. <br><br>This book had me bawling my eyes out the entire time I was reading it. It had me in all kinds of tears: sad tears, happy tears, laughing-so-hard-I'm-gonna-piss-myself tears, you-make-me-so-fucking-angry-I-want-to-choke-you tears - you get the gist. This book made me feel like no other. I have never been so gutted to finish a book. I am on my knees begging for this series to continue, and please please please write her brothers' stories. Lucas, since he's the closest in age to them, and Lachlan - damn, the cutie! I seriously want my own Lachlan. And Little Logan.<br><br>I also can't help but mention, I've never laughed as much as I did in this book while reading a sex scene. Really. Just a heads-up if you've yet to read it. That dialogue - goodness, pure gold!<br><br>I'm not sure, but I think the next book is about Dylan? Please please please. If not Dylan, the Lucas. PLEASE!!!! <i>More Than Enough</i> is its title, and the little "blurb" full of questions has me intrigued. 2015 though :(<br><br>Not being able to read more of their story will be a physical ache for me, so please don't leave me hanging. I NEED MORE OF THEM TO SURVIVE AND CONTINUE ON AS A FUNCTIONING MEMBER OF SOCIETY.<br><br>On the same note, can we please get an extended epilogue for these two? Or a little novella, or something about them in the future?</span>
  <a data-text-id="10099284299206380767" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1804176773" />
    <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie"><img alt="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514769932p2/3275325.jpg" /></a>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1804176773?book_show_action=true">Nov 05, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie">Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ </a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/22711327-more-than-forever">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=kindle-freebies-read">kindle-freebies-read</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=emotional-angsty-books">emotional-angsty-books</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1804176773" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17224597345152173991">4.5 ★'s <br/><blockquote>
  <b> "Because it's eternal, the rise and fall of the sun. It's <i>forever</i>. Just like us." </b>
</blockquote><br/>Having just read <i>Lucas</i> (spin off series from this book), I had to immediately read this one. And just let me warn you...this is filled with angst and it was oh-sooo-good! <br/><br/>In Lucas' book, we find out how happy and in love Lucy and Cameron are but I was really intrigued as to how they got there being so young. I really wasn't prepared for this intense romance at age fifteen!<br/><br/>Cameron coaches baseball for a</span>
  <span id="freeText17224597345152173991" style="display:none">4.5 ★'s <br><blockquote>
  <b> "Because it's eternal, the rise and fall of the sun. It's <i>forever</i>. Just like us." </b>
</blockquote><br>Having just read <i>Lucas</i> (spin off series from this book), I had to immediately read this one. And just let me warn you...this is filled with angst and it was oh-sooo-good! <br><br>In Lucas' book, we find out how happy and in love Lucy and Cameron are but I was really intrigued as to how they got there being so young. I really wasn't prepared for this intense romance at age fifteen!<br><br>Cameron coaches baseball for a couple of Lucy's brothers and he sees her in the bleachers and is immediately smitten. However, Lucy's life takes a tragic turn and when Cameron sees her...he knows <i>exactly</i> where he is needed and just shows up...and keeps showing up. <br><br>Lucy's not too sure about Cameron and what he wants and she can't really spend the time contemplating it. She has her hands full and then some. Cameron makes it easy on her though but it's really their nightly phone calls that connects them. <br><br>A little drama helps put things into perspective. I was really amazed at how "wise" Cameron was and how he keeps coming up with ways to help Lucy. I loved their time at the river and how Lucy was able to pay that forward. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1450982505ra/17494286.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Soon they're in a full fledged relationship but Lucy wants to take the physical side slow which is a good thing. This book is jam packed with so many events and situations that it was good to have something slow! And at fifteen, it was nice to have them wait a bit. That certainly doesn't mean that these two don't experiment. It was funny reading about Cameron being so assured with some things and totally inexperienced with others! <br><br>Thank goodness for Cameron's Mom's boyfriend, Mark. I loved the relationship between Cameron and Mark and all their antics. <br><br>Before I knew, these two were off to college and that's where the real angst started. Holy cow...I knew there would be trouble but I had no idea to the extent. And I don't blame Cameron for any of it except one thing....<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[why, oh why, did he have to draw her? That hurt my heart!  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Well, I could go on and on...I haven't even scratched the surface to what these two go through. Some things weaken them and some strengthen but it is one wild ride. <br><br>I enjoyed getting to know the other couples from the More Than series and if THIS book is close to any of their books, I will be in hog heaven. I've heard Logan's (not Lucas' brother) book is really angsty and I cannot wait!<br><br>I already knew how things worked out but I still loved it all the same. It was a great finish!</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_736467493" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/736467493" />
    <a title="C-Money" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2728874-c-money"><img alt="C-Money" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/736467493?book_show_action=true">Oct 07, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="C-Money" class="user" itemprop="url" name="C-Money" href="/user/show/2728874-c-money">C-Money</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2728874-c-money?shelf=all-time-favorites">all-time-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2728874-c-money?shelf=best-books-ever-written">best-books-ever-written</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2728874-c-money?shelf=6-stars-out-of-this-world">6-stars-out-of-this-world</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer736467493" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11049974691055816960">I look at my life differently now. It is no longer one solid life. It is split up into the BEFORE and the AFTER. When a book is written in such pure form and it changes things, it changes everything about you, you can no longer continue living the life you were before. So now there is BEFORE MTF and AFTER MTF. <br/><br/>I love when a story takes you on a journey. A journey of loss, pain, healing, finding love, doubting yourself and your passion, realizing that life isn't perfect and it won't always be eas</span>
  <span id="freeText11049974691055816960" style="display:none">I look at my life differently now. It is no longer one solid life. It is split up into the BEFORE and the AFTER. When a book is written in such pure form and it changes things, it changes everything about you, you can no longer continue living the life you were before. So now there is BEFORE MTF and AFTER MTF. <br /><br />I love when a story takes you on a journey. A journey of loss, pain, healing, finding love, doubting yourself and your passion, realizing that life isn't perfect and it won't always be easy. It' real and raw and emotional. It is Jay McLean magic at its finest. I don't think a book can get more perfect than More Than Forever. <br /><br />This book was supposed to be about love that will continue on into the FOREVER. But that shit is for the fairy tales. This book, gawd, this book was a roller coaster full of ups and downs. I cried so hard I wanted to vomit. I felt emotion, every ounce of pain. I laid in bed, crying my eyes out, into the early hours of the morning. I couldn't stop, even though the pain was so unbearable at times, I couldn't STOP. <br /><br />There was laughter, there was perma smiles, there was WTF why would you do that? Why would HE do that? Why would SHE do that? I just couldn't understand how a love like theirs, a pure unconditional, knock you off your socks kind of love, has to be tested? <br /><br />Their love started off as young love and what young love lasts? LUCA love last. IT HAS TOO. If their love can't survive the test of time, then what love can? <br /><br />It's not just a story or words on paper. The words become wrapped around your heart, your soul and your very being. They course through your veins and become the reason you breath. That is the only way to really read this book. You have to become one with it, you have to live it and then, only then will you really under stand what MAGIC is. <br /><br />Like every other Jay McLean book, we have get the most amazing side characters. She brings back the old ones that we fell in love with, we get the most amazing parents (one day, hopefully, we will get books about them. I really want a Marky Mark book) and we get more of Lucy's brothers. All of these characters make the book, SO MUCH MORE. They add to the store, they bring it to life right along with Cam and Lucy. That is what good writing is. <br /><br />This is WITH-OUT A DOUBT, THE BEST BOOK EVER WRITTEN BY JAY McLEAN. <br /><br />If the writing world gave OSCARS to characters in a book, CAM and LUCY would be the WINNERS!!!!!<br /><br />Jay McLean you have gone above and beyond the writing world and I am not worthy of your brilliance. You have brought me to my knees and I can't seem to get my ass off the ground. <br /><br />From start to fucking finish this book grabbed me by my invisible balls and might still have a hold of them. <br /><br />Be prepared to have a case of explosives strapped to your chest, because YOU ARE GOING TO BE BLOWN THE FUCK AWAY</span>
  <a data-text-id="11049974691055816960" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer738392255" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7764287854016826412"><br/><b>RE-READ, AND IT MADE ME CRY AGAIN!</b><br/><br/>*Spoiler free*<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1405324263ra/10382154.gif' alt='' height='190' width='380' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1403298394ra/10073171.gif' alt='' height='190' width='380' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1405324263ra/10382155.gif' alt='' height='190' width='380' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1405324263ra/10382156.gif' alt='' height='190' width='380' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>'In a time of nothing but pain, and anger, and emptiness, and hurt... he healed me.<br/>He made it stop. He made it better.<br/>He made me fall in love.'</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><b>Genre:</b> New Adult at it's best<br/><b>Cover:</b> 8/10<br/><b>Writing:</b> 10/10<br/><b>Heroine:</b> 10/10<br/><b>Hero:</b> 9/10<br/><b>Humour:</b> 7/10<br/><b>Hotness:</b> 5/10<br/><b>Romance:</b> 10/10<br/><b>Extra book Details:</b> Approx 390 kindle pages. Dual POV; 1st person. 4th book in the series with different LC's, but you need to read the other books.<br/><br/>If you've read any of the More</span>
  <span id="freeText7764287854016826412" style="display:none"><br><b>RE-READ, AND IT MADE ME CRY AGAIN!</b><br><br>*Spoiler free*<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1405324263ra/10382154.gif" alt="" height="190" width="380" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1403298394ra/10073171.gif" alt="" height="190" width="380" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1405324263ra/10382155.gif" alt="" height="190" width="380" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1405324263ra/10382156.gif" alt="" height="190" width="380" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>'In a time of nothing but pain, and anger, and emptiness, and hurt... he healed me.<br>He made it stop. He made it better.<br>He made me fall in love.'</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><b>Genre:</b> New Adult at it's best<br><b>Cover:</b> 8/10<br><b>Writing:</b> 10/10<br><b>Heroine:</b> 10/10<br><b>Hero:</b> 9/10<br><b>Humour:</b> 7/10<br><b>Hotness:</b> 5/10<br><b>Romance:</b> 10/10<br><b>Extra book Details:</b> Approx 390 kindle pages. Dual POV; 1st person. 4th book in the series with different LC's, but you need to read the other books.<br><br>If you've read any of the More Than series, then you know what you're letting yourself in for;<br><b>High angst, super-sweet romance, lovable characters, big funnies and super sads and an intense love story.<br><br>More Than Forever reached all those expectations and then some.</b><br><br>Lucy and Cam's story starts at the beginning. The very beginning. Cam sees Lucy at her lowest point and can't help but fall in love with her. He's her hero, her strength and her first and only love.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>'I turn around to see her running to me. “Wait!” she yells, and it makes me laugh. Of course I’d wait.<br>I'd wait forever for her.'</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>This is one of those books you just <i>need</i> to read. No description or blurb can explain how good it is. Definitely top dog when it comes to NA. And lately i've been avoiding NA like the plague.<br><br>The characters, bloody hell. I loved them. Mark, what an amazing step-father, seriously, I wanted much more of him, he was awesome.<br><br>Honestly, the feels. I was nearly crying on the page, then the next I was giggling something stupid, only then the flip the page and start bawling. It did <i>that</i> to me. Any book that can make me feel is automatically given a 5 star by me.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>'“You're not an object, I don't want you to think that I own you.”<br>She shrugs. “Why not? I'm yours.”'</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>It's worth it. Totally. I really hated 10% of it. Annoyed, angry, frustrated. But then it went and punched me in the nuts and I made it my favourite of the series.<br><br><b>Super romantic with love epic-ness, dick jokes and the best bunch of characters i've ever read about, this series is a MUST READ.</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="7764287854016826412" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_846467395" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/846467395" />
    <a title="Kelli C " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14931216-kelli-c"><img alt="Kelli C " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1426900480p2/14931216.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/846467395?book_show_action=true">Feb 06, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kelli C " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kelli C " href="/user/show/14931216-kelli-c">Kelli C </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14931216-kelli-c?shelf=amazing">amazing</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14931216-kelli-c?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14931216-kelli-c?shelf=must-reads">must-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14931216-kelli-c?shelf=angst">angst</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14931216-kelli-c?shelf=fab-writing">fab-writing</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14931216-kelli-c?shelf=tear-jerker">tear-jerker</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14931216-kelli-c?shelf=romance-swoon">romance-swoon</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer846467395" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15685113395537141062"><b>A Million Forever Stars.</b><br/><br/>This is by far MY #1 Read of 2014! Without a doubt one of the best series I have ever read. Jay McLean writes young profound love flawlessly. She has created young raunchy humor and pivotal first love feelings perfectly with each book in the More series. However, nothing is as amazing as the story of Cameron and Lucy.<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405281734i/10376402.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>"There is a love so fierce it cannot be measured. A heart so strong it will never slow. there is a promise so sure it can never lie. And we promise that love</b></span>
  <span id="freeText15685113395537141062" style="display:none"><b>A Million Forever Stars.</b><br><br>This is by far MY #1 Read of 2014! Without a doubt one of the best series I have ever read. Jay McLean writes young profound love flawlessly. She has created young raunchy humor and pivotal first love feelings perfectly with each book in the More series. However, nothing is as amazing as the story of Cameron and Lucy.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405281734i/10376402.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>"There is a love so fierce it cannot be measured. A heart so strong it will never slow. there is a promise so sure it can never lie. And we promise that love forever. Forever and always."</b><br><br>Cam and Lucy have been a constant in this series with their "forever" love. It was a pleasure to read where that devotion and emotional connection came from as their tale is so beautifully broken yet so perfect.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405281935i/10376433.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>From the first eye contact at 15, a happy popular Cameron Gordon wanted to "read" a quite withdrawn Lucy. Unlike Cam, Lucy's existence was one of extremes. Taking care of her siblings and father after her mother's death was a difficult feat. Never expecting the big heart of Cameron Gordon to come into her life and literally put her back together. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405282381i/10376486.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>From first kisses and watched sunsets to owning each others pleasure, Jay McLean tells a story of friendship, admiration, and complete consuming passion.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405282381i/10376487.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>I absolutely could not put this book down. There was a consuming power in the story of Cam and Lucy to want a love so deep and so big, yet at the same time, there was no "cheese" or over the top scenes. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1405281681ra/10376394.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>"Because it's more than words spoken, it's his arms around me when I feel like I'm falling. It's his lips on mine, kissing away the pain. It's our hands holding as leads me into the water to let me break. It's us-chest to chest-helping each other heal. It's us-giving each other HOPE."</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405281681i/10376395.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>This was a real love story from start to finish that had bumps and twists in the road to forever, yet every challenge faced just solidified the perfection that was Cam and Lucy...Forever!<br><br><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="15685113395537141062" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('sUMu+LYiETAllv8UZoziUG4uaXAgzIKs2ahQfOBKrgz077UPm8NNXgXsmkx5Qlu1t+ABWGEIFT017nKo1bP6Vw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('gVVmAChYYARMM/CvKzbtCV60yi7XzAdtbYsUyj4z0IHE+f33Bbk8amxJlfc0+FTsh3qiBpYIkPyBzTYeC8qE2g==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>
